NetType:        Direct Allocation

In addition, its interesting reverse looking them up:

For instance:
workspace.google.com has address 142.251.40.206
workspace.google.com has IPv6 address 2607:f8b0:4006:822::200e

bash$ host 142.251.40.206
206.40.251.142.in-addr.arpa domain name pointer lga34s38-in-f14.1e100.net.

bash$ host lga34s38-in-f14.1e100.net
lga34s38-in-f14.1e100.net has address 142.251.40.206
lga34s38-in-f14.1e100.net has IPv6 address 2607:f8b0:4006:822::e
